Arrangements of Certain Officers.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:24.5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On September 25, 2022, Michael G. Van de Ven, President &amp; Chief Operating Officer of Southwest Airlines Co. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;), submitted his resignation from his position of Chief Operating Officer, effective at the end of September 2022, and from his position of President, effective at the end of 2022.  In connection with Mr. Van de Ven&#8217;s resignation, the Board of Directors of the Company (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) unanimously elected Andrew M. Watterson to succeed to the position of Chief Operating Officer, effective October 1, 2022, and Robert E. Jordan to succeed to the position of President, effective January 1, 2023.  Mr. Jordan will also retain his role as the Company&#8217;s Chief Executive Officer.  </span></div><div style="text-indent:24.5pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:24.5pt"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mr. Jordan, age 62, has served as the Company&#8217;s Chief Executive Officer since February 2022 and has been a member of the Board since February 2022. Mr. Jordan also served as Executive Vice President &amp; Incoming Chief Executive Officer from June 2021 to February 2022, Executive Vice President Corporate Services from July 2017 to June 2021, Executive Vice President &amp; Chief Commercial Officer from September 2011 to July 2017, Executive Vice President Strategy &amp; Planning from May 2008 to September 2011, Executive Vice President Strategy &amp; Technology from September 2006 to May 2008, Senior Vice President Enterprise Spend Management from August 2004 to September 2006, Vice President Technology from 2002 to 2004, Vice President Purchasing from 2001 to 2002, Controller from 1997 to 2001, Director Revenue Accounting from 1994 to 1997, and Manager Sales Accounting from 1990 to 1994. Mr. Jordan joined the Company in 1988 as a programmer.</span></div><div style="text-indent:24.5pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:24.5pt"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mr. Watterson, age 55, has served as the Company&#8217;s Executive Vice President &amp; Chief Commercial Officer since January 2020. Mr. Watterson also served as Executive Vice President &amp; Chief Revenue Officer from July 2017 to January 2020, Senior Vice President &amp; Chief Revenue Officer from January 2017 to July 2017, Senior Vice President of Network &amp; Revenue from January 2016 to January 2017, and as Vice President of Network Planning &amp; Performance from October 2013 to January 2016.</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">  </span></div><div style="text-indent:24.5pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:24.5pt"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">In connection with the Board&#8217;s election of Mr. Watterson to serve as Chief Operating Officer, the Compensation Committee of the Board approved an increase in Mr. Watterson&#8217;s annual base salary from $536,700 to $575,000 and an increase in his target cash short-term incentive compensation opportunity from 135 percent of base to 150 percent of base, both effective as of October 1, 2022.</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">  </span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The Company has not entered into, amended, or modified any plan, contract, arrangement, grant, or award in connection with the Board&#8217;s election of Mr. Jordan to serve as President</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">. There are no family relationships between any director or executive officer of the Company and Mr. Jordan or Mr. Watterson. In addition, neither Mr. Jordan nor Mr. Watterson has any relationship requiring disclosure under Item 404 of Regulation S-K, nor is either a party to any arrangement or understanding with any other person pursuant to which he was selected as an officer.  </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div
